 kheti ke jaankaar devinder sharma kehete hai, "bundelkhand jaise ilaakon main jahaan pani ek prachand samasya he vahaan se palaayan hona koi hairaani kii baat nahin he
 In such a situation, organic farming remains an option in which the water requirement is relatively less
 " Jagabhan Kushwaha of Talbehat block used to work for 20 kilometers under NREGA (rural Employment Guarantee Scheme) till 20 years ago, now he is growing vegetables and grains in his fields in an organic way
 jagabhaan bataate hai, "yahaan kisaanon ko bees se pachchis hazaar rupee har maheene kamai is kheti se ho rahi he
 Organic farming has reduced dependence on government schemes like NREGA
 " In Uttar Pradesh, under the NREGA, a wage of Rs 175 is given
 yani har maheene adhiktam kareeb saadhe paanch hazaar rupee kii kamai
 But the problem is that in Bundelkhand, work is not getting under NREGA and the people who get work are paid very late
 upi main naregaa ke liye sangharsh kar rahi sangatin kisaan mazdoor sanghathan kii richa singh kahati hai, "naregaa bahut bure haal main he
 There has been no payment to the workers since 26 January this year
 adhikari hamen bataate hai ki sarkaar ke paas is yojana ke liye koi rakam nahin he
 " jagabhaan bataate hai ki jahaan kaam milane kii sambhaavna hoti he vahaan gram pradhan apane karibiyon or rishtedaaron ko hi kaam dilavaate hai
 In this sense, organic farming is a secure employment for them by leaps and bounds
 tippaniyan The mindless attitude of the weather and the lack of rain in the surrounding areas is also causing trouble for the whole of Bundelkhand
 talbehat block ke karaali gaanv main rahane vaale azaad kehete hai, "zamin main pani kaa jalastr to gir hi rahaa he or agar aasapaas ke ilaakon main bhi barsaat na ho to naharon main pani kii uplabdhta par asar padataa he
 " lekin jaivik kheti se jude kisaanon or saamaajik udhyamiyon kii ek dikkat apane utpaadon ke liye bazaar dhundne kii he
 Organic products are more expensive than chemical farming products and as long as customers are limited to parts of big cities and demand will not increase, this problem is not going to be less
 jaivik kheti ke jaankaar shyaam bihari gupta pichley kai saalon se jaivik utpaadon or graahakon ke bich ek network banane kii koshish main hai
 Shyam Bihari Gupta says, "vegetables, fruits and grains grown organically are expensive
 unhen dilli main hindon yaa yamuna nadi ke kinare nahin ugaaya ja saktaa he kyonki ye to khatarnaak rasayanon se bhari huin hai
 Customers have to understand that when pure products come from 500-600 kilometers away, they will cost a little more
 zehar khaane or paisa dawaaiyon main kharch karne se behatar he thodaa mahangaa lekin surakshit khaanaa khaanaa
 It is also good for a farmer sitting hundreds of kilometers away
 " Farming expert Devinder Sharma says, "it is not surprising that migrating from areas like Bundelkhand where water is a severe problem
 aise main jaivik kheti hi ek vikalp bachataa he jisamen pani kii zarurat apekshaakrit kaaphi kam hoti he
 " talbehat block ke jagabhaan kushvaha do saal pehle tak naregaa (gramin rojgaar guarantee yojana) ke tahat 20 kilometre dur mazaduri karne jate the ab wo jaivik tareeke se apane kheton main subjiyan or anaaj uga rahe hai
 Jagbhan explains, "here farmers are earning twenty to twenty five thousand rupees every month from this farming
 jaivik kheti ne naregaa jaisi sarkari yojana par nirbharta ghatai he
 " uttar pradesh main naregaa ke tahat 175 rupee mazaduri di jaati he
 That is, the maximum earning of about five and a half thousand rupees every month
 lekin samasya ye he ki bundelkhand main naregaa ke tahat kaam nahin mil paa rahaa he or jin logon ko kaam miltaa he unako bhugtan bahut der se hota he
 Richa Singh of Sangitin Kisan Mazdoor Sangathan, who is fighting for NREGA in UP, says, “NREGA is in a very bad condition
 is saal 26 janvari ke baad se mazaduron ko koi bhugtan nahin hua he
 Officials tell us that the government has no funds for this scheme
 " Jagabhan says that where there is a possibility of getting work, the village headmen only get work done to his near and relatives
 is lihaaj se jaivik kheti unke liye kai guna kamai vaala ek surakshit rojgaar he
 The comments mausam ke manamaujee ravaiye or aasapaas ke ilaakon main barsaat na hona bhi puure bundelkhand ke liye pareshaani kaa sabab ban rahaa he
 Azad, who lives in Karali village of Talbehat block, says, "the water level in the land is falling and the availability of water in the canals is affected if there is no rain in the surrounding areas
 " But one of the problems of farmers and social entrepreneurs associated with organic farming is to find a market for their products
 jaivik utpaada rasinic kheti ke utpaadon kii tulana main mahange hote hai or jab tak graahak bade shaharon ke kuch hisson tak simit rahenge or maang nahin badhegi ye dikkat kam hone vaali nahin he
 Organic farming expert Shyam Bihari Gupta has been trying to build a network between organic products and customers for the last several years
 shyaam bihari gupta kehete hai, "jaivik tareeke se ugane vaali sabziyaan, fal or anaaj mahange hote hai
 They cannot be grown on the banks of Hindon or Yamuna in Delhi as they are loaded with hazardous chemicals
 graahakon ko samajhnaa hoga jab shuddh utpaada 500-600 kilometre dur se aaenge to unki keemat thodi adhik hogi
 It is better to eat a little expensive but safe food than eating poison and spending money in medicines
 isse saikadon kilometre dur baithe kisi kisaan kaa bhi bhala hota he

 One such web portal is My Rahat
com and the most important thing about this portal is that this portal has been created by a Kashmiri man and working in his own way for the Kashmiris
 jammu kashmir jaise rajya main jahaan connactivity ek badi baadha he use bazaar kii jad main laana apane aap main ek bada chalange tha or is kaam main mahati bhoomika nibhaa rahe hai kashif or unke dost aabid rashid or jahir hasan
 It is said that in order for any place to develop, it has to be better in terms of health, education and public distribution system
 yourstry
 According to a news on com, Kashif received an engineering degree from Jammu University and started a portal called My Rahat
com to make these fields even better
 iske madhyam se ve sthaneey logon kii gas conection, pashu chikitsa, shiksha samet ve tamaam suvidhaayen kashmiriyon ko dilaane ke liye jammu kashmir mantralay se samanvay banane kii koshish karte hai
 After all, is my relief
com? This is a service whose main purpose is to bring electronic service to the doorsteps of common people
 maay raahat ke uddeshy
 
 
 My Rahat offers its services in 8 key areas such as education, health, agriculture, news, media, utilities, products, e-governance and travel
 iske alaava ve kaisamaajik udhyamonke saath sambandhon ke kii sthapana kii he
 They are trying to set up companies and businesses operating within the state, creating a platform for the government and most importantly, providing employment to Kashmiri youth
 ve sarkaar or kashmiri yuvaaon ke bich pul kaa kaam kar rahe hai
 They are trying to connect the youth living in those rural areas and deprived of basic facilities with this portal
 ve bataate hai ki is seva ke liye graahak ko 300 se 500 rupee kharch karne hote hai or aaj is portal se jude graahakon kii sankhya 1,500 pahunch chuki he
 In the meantime, they have tied up with 30 institutions and are helping all the rural and marginalized people of the state at very low prices
 aaj unke portal se pratidin phayda uthaane vaale logon kii sankhya 1000 he or is bich hi unhone 1 million kaa aankada chuaa he

 kashif apane is sakaaratmak prayaas se kashmir kii vaadiyon main khushi bikherne kaa kaam kar rahe hai
